integrations. This reviewer was not provided any incentive by G2 for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Review source: In-app</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-8"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2022-02-02" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2022-02-02">Feb 02, 2022</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/impact-com-performance/reviews/impact-com-performance-review-5313465"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"User-freindly, clean interface for publishers"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Impact.com has built relationships with highly recognizable brands that draw shoppers' attention.  Getting links to advertisers is easy. Compared to competitors, Impact.com has a great dashboard that summarizes everything I need to see. I am most interested in transactions that have occurred, rather than new merchants, and Impact.com focuses on showing traffic first. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Searching for new brands is a little buried. Also, our company has created dynamic links where we capture a user's username and embed it into a sub-field. It was challenging to know which report to pull where this value was shown, so maybe a description of each report would be helpful. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5313465 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">It is quite difficult to build a direct relationship with a big brand merchant. Our platform allows you to shop at participating merchants and generate a donation to your charity of choice. Without Impact.com, our participating merchant list would not be as impressive. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex The advertisers are within my niche, and therefore, I can convert sales more efficiently. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The impact.com interface, while it has a lot of great features, can be a bit clunky to use.  The sign-out button is in the bottom left corner.  Please put it in the top right corner like everyone else.  And I have not been able to figure out how to withdraw an application if an advertiser does not answer my request within a reasonable time.  I think the withdraw button shows up after x number of days, but you have to hunt for it. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5339172 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The biggest problem is getting the right advertisers and converting clicks to sales.  impact.com has a good mix of advertisers, and my sales have been decent, though they always could be better. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" Everyone loves wireless earbuds because it allows them to listen to music on the go, but only if it's the Apple AirPods. Impact gives me the incentive to want to review different brands of earbuds because all I need to do to make money selling those items is use Impact to create links to them. <span class="spht">Review
